These are formatted for forum use. [img=https://retroachievements.org/Images/labels/linkedfiles.png'] can 
be posted at the top of the list. Roms used to make the set can be labeled using 
[img=https://retroachievements.org/Images/labels/main.png] Standard placement is between the [b] 
and the filename. Entries that have more than one rom linked may be numbered for 
clarity. You may look up existing forum posts for reference. 

Hashes are included mainly to make it easier to find the proper entry. It would 
probably be better to copy only the first two lines of each entry since the hash 
only relates to what hash the emulator recognizes and does not actually indicate 
anything about the file or compatibility. Neo geo games are listed as parent sets 
even though they require the proper neogeo bios and are considered its children.

Current version for compatibility corresponds to the FB Alpha v0.2.97.43. While 
mame is updated every month (not currently supported) FBA was recently updated 
after some years from FB Alpha v0.2.97.42. Some parent roms have been updated 
since then and librretro has updated its core in the last few months to support 
v0.2.97.43, so make sure you have the latest version of the set for compatibility. 
If at some point in the future FBA is updated, you may need to replace old files 
once the core is updated as well to maintain compatibility.
